</th>

<span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_oboe&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the oboe</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="17 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_clarinet&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the clarinet</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Serenade for Wind Instruments
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Serenáda pro dechové nástroje
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Dvo%C5%99%C3%A1k,_Anton%C3%ADn" title="Category:Dvořák, Antonín">Dvořák, Antonín</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.44, B.77
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IAD 79
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>D minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 movements:
<ol><li> Moderato quasi marcia (D minor)
</li><li> Tempo di minuet (F major) - Trio. Presto (B-flat major)
</li><li> Andante con moto (A major)
</li><li> Finale: Allegro molto (D minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1878
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1878-11-17 in Prague
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1879 - Berlin: <a href="/wiki/N._Simrock" title="N. Simrock">N. Simrock</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Ehlert,_Louis" title="Category:Ehlert, Louis">Louis Ehlert</a>&#160;(1825-1884)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>25 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons, contrabassoon, 3 horns, cello, double bass
</td></tr>
